(August 20, 2020) &#8211;&#8211; The Cato Corporation (NYSE: CATO)<div style="display:inline-block;width:6.15px">&#160;</div>today reported a net </div><div id="a143" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:384.2px;">loss of $7.2 million or ($0.30) per diluted share for the second quarter ended August 1, 2020, </div><div id="a177" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:411.9px;">compared to net income of $11.9<div style="display:inline-block;width:5.73px">&#160;</div>million or $0.48 per diluted share for the second quarter ended </div><div id="a211" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:439.4px;">August 3, 2019.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.06px">&#160;</div>Sales for the second quarter were $166.3 million, or a decrease of 21% from sales </div><div id="a248" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:467.1px;">of $210.4 million for the second quarter ended August 3, 2019.<div style="display:inline-block;width:13.44px">&#160;</div>The Company&#8217;s same-store sales for </div><div id="a282" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:494.6px;">the quarter decreased 24% to the same period last year. </div><div id="a302" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:530.3px;">As previously announced Cato closed all stores due to the COVID-19 pandemic beginning March 19, </div><div id="a334" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:557.8px;">2020.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.11px">&#160;</div>On May 1, 2020, the Company began reopening stores in a phased approach, with limited </div><div id="a367" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:585.5px;">operating hours, consistent with local health and safety guidelines and regulations.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.13px">&#160;</div>As of June 15, </div><div id="a397" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:613px;">2020, all stores had reopened. </div><div id="a407" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:648.7px;">For the six months ended August 1, 2020, the Company reported a net loss of $35.6 million or ($1.48) </div><div id="a445" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:676.2px;">per diluted share, compared to net income of $33.1 million or $1.34 per diluted share for the six </div><div id="a481" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:703.9px;">months ended August 3, 2019.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.17px">&#160;</div>Sales for the six months ended August 1, 2020 were $265.1 million, </div><div id="a515" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:731.4px;">down 40% to sales of $438.4 million for the six months ended August 3, 2019.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.12px">&#160;</div>Year<div style="display:inline-block;width:1.47px">&#160;</div>-to-date same-</div><div id="a553" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:759.1px;">store sales decreased 39%. </div><div id="a561" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:786.6px;">&#8220;Sales softened through the quarter and into early August.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.16px">&#160;</div>As we<div style="display:inline-block;width:4.43px">&#160;</div>see this trend continuing, we are </div><div id="a596" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:814.3px;">cautious about the second half of the year,&#8221; stated John Cato, Chairman, President, and Chief </div><div id="a626" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:841.9px;">Executive Officer.<div style="display:inline-block;width:10.22px">&#160;</div>&#8220;And we remain committed to protecting our customers, associates and the </div><div id="a652" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:869.4px;">communities we serve, in light of the unprecedented situation regarding the COVID-19 pandemic.&#8221;<div style="display:inline-block;width:4.67px">&#160;</div></div></div>
</div>

decreased to 20.2% from 38.0% of sales in the quarter, due to a reduction in </div><div id="a742" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:91px;">merchandise contribution, combined with the effects of deleveraging from the sales decline related to </div><div id="a771" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:118.7px;">the phased reopening of stores and limited operating to 26.4% from 31.4% during the quarter primarily due to company-wide expense reduction </div><div id="a834" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:173.9px;">initiatives and elimination of incentive compensation.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.26px">&#160;</div>A pre-tax loss and the beneficial effects of the </div><div id="a866" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:201.4px;">CARES Act resulted in $3.9 million tax benefit versus $2.1 million expense in the prior year.<div style="display:inline-block;width:10px">&#160;</div>During </div><div id="a900" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:229.1px;">the quarter, the Company paid $30 million on its line of credit, bringing the outstanding balance to $0.<div style="display:inline-block;width:5.58px">&#160;</div></div><div id="a937" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:256.6px;">The Company ended the quarter with unrestricted cash and short-term investments of $137.0 million </div><div id="a967" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:284.3px;">and full availability on its $35 million revolving line of credit.<div style="display:inline-block;width:4.75px">&#160;</div></div><div id="a990" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:327.8px;">Year<div style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:355.6px;">reduction in merchandise contribution combined with the effects of deleveraging resulting from the </div><div id="a1054" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:383.1px;">sales decline.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9px">&#160;</div>The year-to-date SG&amp;A rate was 36.4% versus 30.0% last year primarily due to the </div><div id="a1090" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:410.8px;">effects of deleveraging and store impairment charges of $5.3 million, partially offset by company-wide </div><div id="a1120" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:438.3px;">expense reductions and the elimination of incentive compensation.<div compared to an expense of $6.4 million last year. </div><div id="a1175" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:509.5px;">During the second quarter ended August 1, 2020, the Company opened 36 new stores which were </div><div id="a1207" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:537.2px;">previously committed, relocated 1 store and permanently closed 3 stores.<div states, compared to 1,299 stores in 31 states as of August 3, </div><div id="a1275" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:592.4px;">2019. </div><div id="a1277"
